# Parity Change Log

## [v1.6.6](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/releases/v1.6.6) (2017-04-11)
[Full Changelog](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/compare/v1.6.5...v1.6.6)

**Enhancements:**

- Replace `minBlock` property on `eth\_sendTransaction` Transaction parameter in documentation with `condition` property. [\#5391](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/5391) [[F5-documentation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F5-documentation)] [[M6-rpcapi](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/M6-rpcapi)]

- Tx progress should display tokens in the case of token transfers [\#5315](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/5315) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[M7-ui](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/M7-ui)]

- Poll nonces for light client transaction queue senders periodically [\#5012](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/5012) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[M4-core](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/M4-core)]

- Handle migrations which simply add columns [\#4581](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/4581) [[F7-optimisation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F7-optimisation)] [[M4-core](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/M4-core)]

- RPC trace\_replayTransaction for stateDiff crashes Parity for some transactions [\#2600](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/2600) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)] [[P2-asap](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P2-asap)]

**Closed issues:**

- Address already in use [\#2621](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/2621)

## [v1.2.2](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/releases/v1.2.2) (2016-07-16)
[Full Changelog](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/compare/v1.2.1...v1.2.2)

**Enhancements:**

- Find simple transactions [\#1606](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1606) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]
- Replace locks with parking\_lot alternatives [\#1374](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1374) [[F7-optimisation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F7-optimisation)] [[P7-nicetohave](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P7-nicetohave)]
- Minimise calls to update sealing [\#1372](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1372) [[F7-optimisation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F7-optimisation)]
- Passive operating modes [\#1244](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1244) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]

**Fixed bugs:**

- Backport \#1548 to beta [\#1617](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1617) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- getBlockByNumber\("latest"\) and getBlockByNumber\("pending"\) return the same block [\#1564](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1564) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- parity daemon should log to file [\#1560](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1560) [[F3-annoyance](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F3-annoyance)]
- Network crash on start/stop [\#1553](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1553) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Transactions are removed from queue when gas limit is reached [\#1544](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1544) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Corrupted DB after reboot [\#1535](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1535) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Windows 10 UI Missing Fonts  [\#1529](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1529) [[F3-annoyance](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F3-annoyance)]

- Failing build on rust beta [\#1520](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1520) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Set a timeout for ETH price lookup [\#1519](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1519) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- More descriptive RPC error responses. [\#1114](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1114) [[F3-annoyance](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F3-annoyance)] [[P7-nicetohave](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P7-nicetohave)]

## [v1.2.1](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/releases/v1.2.1) (2016-07-01)
[Full Changelog](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/compare/v1.2.0...v1.2.1)

**Enhancements:**

- Send block to all peers if we mined it [\#1473](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1473) [[F7-optimisation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F7-optimisation)]
- New block mined log output [\#1468](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1468) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P7-nicetohave](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P7-nicetohave)]
- Optional max gas for transactions [\#1456](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1456) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P5-sometimesoon](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P5-sometimesoon)]
- Add an option to disable transaction sealing updates [\#1447](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1447) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]
- Make db settings adjustable via cli [\#1446](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1446) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P5-sometimesoon](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P5-sometimesoon)]
- Attempt to recover DB after corruption [\#1367](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1367) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]
- Mist Wallet wallet-contract creation broken [\#1332](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1332) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]
- Mining should not start until initial full sync is complete. [\#1056](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1056) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P9-somedaymaybe](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P9-somedaymaybe)]
- Mined block should be short-cutted into the chain [\#773](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/773) [[F7-optimisation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F7-optimisation)] [[P9-somedaymaybe](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P9-somedaymaybe)]
- Try to recover a rocksdb database corrupted from out of disk [\#763](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/763) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P7-nicetohave](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P7-nicetohave)]
- Database rescue [\#165](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/165) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)] [[P9-somedaymaybe](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P9-somedaymaybe)]

**Fixed bugs:**

- Websockets module panics on Ctrl-C [\#1462](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1462) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- fill\_optional\_fields not supplying default value 0 [\#1458](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1458) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Crash in MIO on connection aborted. [\#1449](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1449) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Signer panics when port is not available. [\#1448](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1448) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Sync failed. [\#1442](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1442) [[F0-consensus](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F0-consensus)]
-  --signer blocks "Address is already in use" message [\#1439](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1439) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Windows: Node's web3.js fails to connect to parity JSONRPC [\#1438](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1438) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- parity taking 100% CPU [\#1435](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1435) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)] [[P2-asap](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P2-asap)]
- Database error results in opaque UTF-8 encoding panic [\#1434](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1434) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)] [[P5-sometimesoon](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P5-sometimesoon)]
- Ctrl-C causes panic in ethcore\_signer [\#1433](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/1433) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]

**Enhancements:**

- installation of multirust shouldn't be with sudo [\#942](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/942) [[F5-documentation](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F5-documentation)]

## [v1.0.2](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/releases/v1.0.2) (2016-04-11)
[Full Changelog](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/compare/v1.0.1...v1.0.2)

**Enhancements:**

- JSONRPC should be able to handle a large number of connections [\#799](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/799) [[F8-enhancement](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F8-enhancement)]

**Fixed bugs:**

- Directory for --keys-path is not created [\#911](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/911) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- eth\_getFilterChanges Must return events since the last poll [\#909](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/909) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Panicked syncing [\#902](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/902) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Events/logs don't work in parity's RPC [\#895](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/895) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- eth\_call broken. [\#887](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/887) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Parity does not work with contracts: [\#885](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/885) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- --keys-path not working as expected [\#882](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/882) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Take nonce from TransactionQueue at a preference to BlockChain [\#875](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/875) [[F3-annoyance](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F3-annoyance)]
- Syncing stops sometimes [\#873](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/873) [[F0-consensus](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F0-consensus)]
- Mac OS X - Geth keys not imported/visible [\#869](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/869) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Official AMD64 binary SIGILL crash [\#861](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/861) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Contract creation using web3 doesn't give return address [\#855](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/855) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Some threads continue to run in background after Ctrl-C causing panic on re-run [\#848](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/848) [[F2-bug](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F2-bug)]
- Sync sometimes stops on bad block \(morden chain\) [\#827](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/827) [[F0-consensus](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F0-consensus)] [[P2-asap](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/P2-asap)]
- Switch to using hyper mio branch  [\#823](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/823) [[F3-annoyance](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F3-annoyance)]

**Closed issues:**

- Ctrl-c causes some threads to panic. [\#896](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/896)
- Syncing "hangs" on ARM [\#868](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/868)

**Enhancements:**

- Box up JournalDB to allow multiple implementations [\#672](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/issues/672) [[F6-refactor](https://github.com/paritytech/parity/labels/F6-refactor)]
